  1  	"""
  2  	Returns total price paid for individual rentals
  3  ->	"""
  4  	import argparse
  5  	import json
  6  	import datetime
  7  	import math
  8
  9
 10  	def parse_cmd_arguments():
 11  	    """ Parse arguments from cmdline """
 12  	    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='Process some integers.')
 13  	    parser.add_argument('-i',
 14  	                        '--input',
 15  	                        help='input JSON file',
 16  	                        required=True)
 17  	    parser.add_argument('-o',
 18  	                        '--output',
 19  	                        help='ouput JSON file',
 20  	                        required=True)
 21
 22  	    return parser.parse_args()
 23
 24
 25  	def load_rentals_file(filename):
 26  	    """ Load into JSON rental file """
 27  	    with open(filename) as file:
 28  	        try:
 29  	            data = json.load(file)
 30  	        except ValueError:
 31  	            exit(0)
 32  	    return data
 33
 34
 35  	def calculate_additional_fields(data):
 36  	    """ Calculate cost and return data dict """
 37  	    for value in data.values():
 38  	        try:
 39  	            rental_start = datetime.datetime.strptime(
 40  	                value['rental_start'], '%m/%d/%y')
 41  	            rental_end = datetime.datetime.strptime(
 42  	                value['rental_end'], '%m/%d/%y')
 43  	            value['total_days'] = abs((rental_end - rental_start).days)
 44  	            value['total_price'] = value['total_days'] * value['price_per_day']
 45  	            value['sqrt_total_price'] = math.sqrt(value['total_price'])
 46  	            value['unit_cost'] = value['total_price'] / value['units_rented']
 47  	        except Exception as e:
 48  	            print(e)
 49  	            exit(0)
 50
 51  	    return data
 52
 53
 54  	def save_to_json(filename, data):
 55  	    """ Save data to JSON file """
 56  	    with open(filename, 'w') as file:
 57  	        json.dump(data, file)
 58
 59  	if __name__ == "__main__":
 60  	    args = parse_cmd_arguments()
 61 B	    data = load_rentals_file(args.input)
 62  	    data = calculate_additional_fields(data)
 63  	    save_to_json(args.output, data)

  9
 10  	def parse_cmd_arguments():
 11  	    """ Parse arguments from cmdline """
 12  	    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='Process some integers.')
 13  	    parser.add_argument('-i',
 14  	                        '--input',
 15  	                        help='input JSON file',
 16  	                        required=True)
 17  	    parser.add_argument('-o',
 18  	                        '--output',
 19  	                        help='ouput JSON file',
 20  	                        required=True)
 21
 22  	    return parser.parse_args()
 23
 24
 25  	def load_rentals_file(filename):
 26  	    """ Load into JSON rental file """
 27  	    with open(filename) as file:
 28  	        try:
 29  	            data = json.load(file)
 30  	        except ValueError:
 31  	            exit(0)
 32  	    return data
 33
 34
 35  	def calculate_additional_fields(data):
 36  	    """ Calculate cost and return data dict """
 37  	    for value in data.values():
 38  	        try:
 39  	            rental_start = datetime.datetime.strptime(
 40  	                value['rental_start'], '%m/%d/%y')
 41  	            rental_end = datetime.datetime.strptime(
 42  	                value['rental_end'], '%m/%d/%y')
 43  	            value['total_days'] = abs((rental_end - rental_start).days)
 44  	            value['total_price'] = value['total_days'] * value['price_per_day']
 45  	            value['sqrt_total_price'] = math.sqrt(value['total_price'])
 46  	            value['unit_cost'] = value['total_price'] / value['units_rented']
 47  	        except Exception as e:
 48  	            print(e)
 49  	            exit(0)
 50
 51  	    return data
 52
 53
 54  	def save_to_json(filename, data):
 55  	    """ Save data to JSON file """
 56  	    with open(filename, 'w') as file:
 57  	        json.dump(data, file)
 58
 59  	if __name__ == "__main__":
 60  	    args = parse_cmd_arguments()
 61  	    data = load_rentals_file(args.input)
 62 B	    data = calculate_additional_fields(data)
 63  	    save_to_json(args.output, data)
